name:A‍n‍o‍n‍y‍m‍o‍u‍s‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Deluxe Queen Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:38 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:This time, the family traveled and stayed at Zhangjiakou International Hotel, which was a good experience:
The hotel is antique, and the facade, lobby, and corridor are very grand. There are mostly office buildings around, adjacent to the park, and the hotel is clean, tidy, and relatively quiet. The room is decorated in an old-style hotel, but the king-size room is spacious, with a bathtub and a refrigerator, and fruits, yogurt, and small biscuits are delivered to the room at night.
The hotel has four restaurants: Chinese restaurant, Vietnamese restaurant, Japanese restaurant, and Dian Yuede Tea Restaurant. When I went there, it happened to be a beer festival in the hotel, and there was an open-air barbecue in the small square in front of the hotel at night.
On the first day of check-in, I tasted the Yueshe restaurant on the first floor for dinner. The environment was very good. Four people spent 370 yuan, and the Tom Yum soup tasted good.
Breakfast is on the second floor, with Cantonese morning tea, Inner Mongolian morning tea, Western bread and cakes, etc., as well as some other things such as pancakes, wontons, etc. The dishes are rich, and the waiters are also very enthusiastic and will take the initiative to help guests in need, such as giving pregnant women a backrest.
Because a family member had a birthday during the trip, we booked a birthday banquet in the hotel's Chinese restaurant. The restaurant was very creatively decorated and we liked it very much. We can see that the hotel is very attentive. The acrostic poems based on the guests' names were displayed on the TV, on napkins, and even on the yogurt we drank. There was also a small interaction during the cake session, and the dishes tasted quite good. When I returned to the room, I unexpectedly found that there were also happy birthday candles and flowers in the room, and framed photos were given as gifts.
Especially the clean and hygienic guest rooms, the bright windows and clean tables, the thoughtful and meticulous service, I felt at home.
Overall, I was very satisfied and the service was super five-star praise. I will consider coming again.

The room is nice, the bathroom is large and has a bathtub. The shower has enough hot water and the room has no noise or smell. The bed is made up of two single beds and is huge enough to be used as a kang.

The best thing is the breakfast. The buffet is very rich. Both Chinese and Western styles are available. There are regular salads, stir-fries, noodles, sausages, toast, and Cantonese-style seafood porridge, which tastes authentic. There are pancakes on site, and milk tea is also delicious There's even lamb soup with haggis.
The swimming pool is average and slightly small. There are also training classes and there are many people.
The hotel has a large courtyard. In the summer, there are hotel-operated food stalls in the courtyard. It is recommended to try it. It is very good and there is also a band singing. It is recommended to eat the freshly grilled mutton skewers, delicious!
There is a charging pile in the hotel yard, which is the fast charging pile of Camax, but the plug of this brand is special and some cars cannot be plugged in. If there is a situation where charging cannot be done, there is a special call from the ground parking lot of Times Square next to it, and the parking lot is 6 yuan each Hour.

第二彈：接下來房間升級，贈送梨汁和水果，前台和客房的服務人員很熱情。
第三彈：晚餐在一層越南風味餐廳很有異國情調，院外散步看到户外燒烤和樂隊演出，羊肉串是現場穿的，大堂有鋼琴演奏。
第四彈：房間乾淨，枕頭舒服，花灑水量大，門和窗户隔音，窗簾隔光。
第五彈：早餐本想吃個雞蛋喝口熱湯，沒想到把我驚艷了，餐廳裝修時尚顏色明快，菜品有張家口風味、廣東早茶以及一些西餐，菜品豐富，味道不錯，服務人員不多，但井然有序。
第六彈：中午本來延至兩點，但有事耽擱回來時略晚，前台服務員説別著急，沒事，晚個10分8分沒關係，瞬間對酒店的好感又多了幾分。
總之，這是一家值得再去的酒店。
